*Grade 1 Maths — January Quiz*
_2054 questions (1554 new + 500 revision)_

*Q1.* 🕐 Tara's class begins at 3 o'clock. What time is 1 hour later?
A) 4 o'clock
B) 3 o'clock
C) 5 o'clock
D) 2 o'clock
✅ *Answer:* A) 4 o'clock
💡 One hour after 3 o'clock is 4 o'clock.
━━━━━━━━━━
*Q2.* 🖐️ Skip count by 5s: 32, 37, 42, __?
A) 47
B) 42
C) 46
D) 48
✅ *Answer:* A) 47
💡 Adding 5 each time, next is 47.
━━━━━━━━━━
*Q3.* 🧮 A sharpener costs ₹7 and a pen costs ₹10. How much MORE does the costlier one cost?
A) ₹4
B) ₹2
C) ₹3
D) ₹5
✅ *Answer:* C) ₹3
💡 ₹10 - ₹7 = ₹3.
━━━━━━━━━━

C) 31
D) 1
✅ *Answer:* A) 41
💡 41 is the greatest.
